        "question": "Write a paragraph about 'A Tea Stall'. Answer the following questions in your paragraph.\n\na) What is a tea stall? b) Where is it generally found? c) How is a tea stall decorated? d) What things are sold here? e) What is the condition of a tea stall? f) What do the customers do here?",
        "solution": "[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math]A Tea StallA tea stall is a roadside shop for people who go there to have tea as well as other snacks. A tea stall is very common both in towns and villages in our country. It usually sits in a crowded place. It is found in a marketplace, a square, a bus stand, a railway station and near schools and colleges. In a tea stall, usually, tea is served to the customers in exchange for money. But biscuits, bananas, cigarettes, betel leaves, etc. are also sold there. Though some tea stalls are well-furnished, most of them are poorly furnished. It is usually decorated with chairs, tables and benches. People go to a tea stall to take a cup of tea to remove their tiredness. A tea stall is kept open from early morning till late night. In a tea stall, there are generally two people to manage and run it. One is a grown-up man who prepares tea and takes the bill from the customers, and the other is a young boy who serves tea, biscuits, etc. to the customers. Sometimes, people go to a tea stall in a group and raise a storm over the cup. They discusspolitics, daily affairs, various problems and what not. After all, a tea stall is a useful place for many people.Word Meaning: snacks হালকা খাবার; crowded -জনাকীর্ণ; decorated – সাজানো; remove দূর করা; tiredness ক্লান্তি: customers - ক্রেতা/খারদ্দার; well-furnished - সুসজ্জিত; raise তোলা; storm - ঝড়; daily affairs দৈনন্দিন বিষয়াবলী।",

        "solution": "[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] Our School MagazineA school magazine is a periodical publication that contains the literary works and other information of a school. It is published once a year. We have a school magazine in our school. To publish it smoothly, a magazine committee of usually nine members is formed in a general meeting. The members of the committee are chief patron, adviser, editor, assistant editors, business editors, proofreaders, assistant proofreaders, etc. The Headteacher holds the post of chief patron and a senior teacher becomes the adviser. The editor, business editors and the assistant proofreaders are selected from the students. A magazine fund is also made up from the school 'Magazine Fee'. The editor invites writings both in Bangla and English. Then, after proper scrutiny, the best ones are selected for publishing. The business editors collect some money by selling spaces in the magazine for advertisements. Generally, the magazine has two sections- Bangla and English. There are messages from the Headteacher and the Secretary of the school. There are also annual reports, essays, short stories, short plays, etc. in it. It also contains jokes, quizes and puzzles. Most of the articles are written by the students. A few articles are written by the teachers. A school magazine promoting team-spirit inspires to express the dormant power of thinking as well as writing of the young learners. It helps flourish themselves as future writers and poets.Word Meaning: contain (v) - ধারণ করা/থাকা; literary (adj) সাহিত্য বিষয়ক; information (n) – তথ্য; smoothly (adv) - মসৃণভাবে; form (v) - গঠন করা; patron (n) পৃষ্ঠপোষক; adviser (n) - উপদেষ্টা; editor (n) সম্পাদক; invite (v) - আহ্বান করা; proper (adj) - যথাযথ; scrutiny (n) বিচার বিশ্লেষণ; select (v) নির্বাচন করা; collect (v) সংগ্রহ করা; promote (v) - উন্নীত করা/প্রচার করা; inspire (v) অনুপ্রাণিত করা; express (v) প্রকাশ করা; flourish (v) - বিকশিত করা।",

        "question": "Write a paragraph on 'The Life of a Farmer' by answering the following questions.\n\na) Who is a farmer? b) When does he start his daily work? c) How does he lead his life? d) What is his contribution to the nation? e) How can we improve his condition?",
        "solution": "[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] Our School MagazineAny person who is involved in the cultivation of crops, or livestock is called a farmer. He gets up early in the morning and starts his daily works. Generally, a farmer is a poor man. Most of the farmers have no land of their own. So, he cultivates the land of others. He lives from hand to mouth. He works very hard to prepare the land for planting or sowing crops. From the farmers' growing and reaping the harvest, we can have our food. By working hard in the field, he grows a bumper crop which helps to develop our national economy. We know that our country is an agricultural country. More than 80 percent people are directly or indirectly engaged in agriculture. Our economy is also mostly dependent on it. So, to promote the development of the national economy, the farmers should be helped with agricultural subsidies by the government. They should be encouraged to use tractors instead of the age-old ploughs. They should also be taught to use modern cultivation methods. This is how the farmers can be developed.Word Meaning: land জমি; prepare প্রস্তুত করা; crops ফসল; bumper ব্যাপক; economy অর্থনীতি; agricultural কৃষিপ্রধান; directly প্রত্যক্ষভাবে; dependent নির্ভরশীল; subsidies ভর্তুকি; instead পরিবর্তে; modern আধুনিক; cultivation - চাষাবাদ; methods - পদ্ধতি।",

How do the animals and birds pass this day? (d) What do the children do on this day? (e) How do you pass the day?",
        "solution": "[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] A Rainy DayA rainy day is dull and gloomy. Sometimes, it drizzles and sometimes, it rains heavily all day long. The sky remains overcast with black clouds. The sun is hardly visible. Gusty wind blows from all sides. Birds keep standing on branches of trees or keep quiet in their nests. Cattle remain in their sheds and bellow for the fodder. Water stands here and there. Unpitched roads become muddy and slippery. Passers-by have to walk with umbrella over their head, shoes in hand and pants folded up to the knee. Sometimes people slip and fall on the muddy road. In cities, a rainy day is now a horror. The roads and streets in some towns and cities get flooded. Vehicles are seen stranding in knee-deep water in some areas due to water clogging. It causes gridlock across the city. It is a day of trouble and annoyance to the office-going people. They have to suffer from various inconveniences. But for the school going children, it is a delight to have a rainy day. If it rains heavily before their school time, they get a holiday. Sometimes, children, especially the boys play football in the rainwater in the nearby fields. A rainy day is a curse for the poor. The day labourers cannot go out for work and hence, they have to suffer a lot. However, I pass the day by listening to music, watching TV or reading journals. In short, a rainy day is a a day of both pleasure and pain.Word Meaning: dull and gloomy (phr) – নিষ্প্রভ এবং বিষণ্ণ; drizzle (v) গুঁড়ি গুঁড়ি বৃষ্টি হওয়া; overcast (adj) – মেঘাচ্ছন্ন; visible (adj) - দৃশ্যমান; gusty (adj) ঝড়ো; fodder (n) গবাদি পশুর শুকনা খাদ্য; water clogging (phr) – জলাবদ্ধতা; annoyance (n) - বিরক্তি; inconvenience (n) - অসুবিধা; journal (n) সংবাদপত্র/সাময়িক পত্র; In short (phr) - এক কথায়/সংক্ষেপে।",

        "question": "Answer the following questions to write a paragraph on \"Tree plantation\":\n\n(a) What does a tree do for us?\n\n(b) What happens if there were no trees?\n\n(c) What is the effect of the loss of trees?\n\n(d) What should be done to save mankind?\n\n(e) How can be made the earth greener, cleaner and safer?\n\n(f) What part do people play in protecting trees and increasing forests?",
        "solution": "[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] Tree Plantation (বৃক্ষরোপণ)Nowadays \"tree plantation' has become a much ventilated issue. \"Tree plantation' means planting trees in a large number to prevent deforestation. The importance of tree plantation beggars description. Firstly, trees provide us with various fruits, honey, fodder for animals, and medicine. Secondly, they supply timber which is used in housing, in making furniture, toys and vehicles, and in manufacturing paper and pencils. Thirdly. almost all the birds and many animals depend on trees for their habitat. Fourthly, trees play the key-role in protecting our environment and maintaining ecological balance. They prevent erosion of soil and protect houses from flood and storm. They absorb carbon-di-oxide, a major culprit for green-house effect. They help rain to occur. Random felling of trees may cause rapid desertification. In recent times, the importance of tree plantation is being desperately felt because our environment is facing increasing threats day by day. Temperature is ever on the rise; polar ice is melting and sea-level is rising; yield of crops are collapsing and so on. July and August are the best time for tree plantation. To motivate people for tree plantation, mass-awareness should be raised.         "options": [],
        "question": "Answering the following questions to write a paragraph on 'Water Pollution' :\n\n(a) What is water pollution?\n\n(b) Why is water called life?\n\n(c) How is water polluted?\n\n(d) What are the effects of water pollution?\n\n(e) What measures should we take to prevent water pollution?",
        "solution": "Water is an essential element of environment. No one can live without water. This is why water is called life. But nowadays it is being polluted in many ways. This pollution of water through various ways is called water pollution. Different kinds of human waste fall into water through unplanned drainage system. Chemicals and fertilizers used by farmers and industrial waste pollute water. Engine vehicles using fossil fuels ply the rivers and seas, and leave oil and waste materials into water. As a result, water is polluted. Thermal pollution and radio-active wastage are also responsible. The effects of water pollution are numerous because it triggers imbalance in the entire environment and becomes the cause of many diseases. Every year diarrhoea, cholera, typhoid and such other diseases breaking out as a result of water pollution cause millions of deaths in the world. To prevent water pollution, we should leave no stone unturned and have to check all the culprits responsible for it. Proper dumping of all sorts of waste is the most effective step here. Sanitary latrines should be introduced widely in the river-side areas. Passing as well as enforcing a law against dumping of waste into water is sure to be fruitful. A tea stall is found at a market place, a square, a bus stand, a railway station and near schools and colleges. Though some stalls are well fumished, most of the tea stalls are poorly furnished with furniture. People go to a tea stall to take a cup of tea in order to remove tiredness. Load-shedding occurs witen supply of electricity is less than the demand. Unplanned distribution is also responsible. Load-shedding hampers us in many ways. Mills, factories, houses, hospitals, shops etc, all fall victims to load-shedding. Failure of electricity hampers productivity in factories and industries. Medical operations are stopped. Food-items kept in refrigerators get rotten. Commodities kept in cold-storages get spoiled. Load-shedding at night causes greater problems. Housewives in the kitchen grope in the darkness. Students have to sit idly closing their books. The deplorable plight of the sick and the old beggars description on a hot summer day when electricity goes off. To cope with the situation created by load-shedding, candles, charge lights, IPS etc, can be used. To get rid of load-shedding, all necessary steps should be taken to produce the needed amount of electricity and ensure proper distribution.\n\nSelected Vocabulary (নির্ধারিত শব্দার্থ): Phenomenonঘটনা, বিষn discontinuation-feuren, victim-fon commodities-দ্রব্যসামী: spoil- নষ্ট করা deplorable শোচনীয়: beggar description কর্ণনাতীত হওয়া। plight শোচনীয় অবস্থা, দূরবস্থা। IPS-Instant Power Supply জরুরি (বিদ্যুৎ) শক্তি সরবরাহ, distribution কটন grope হাতড়ানো, অন্ধের মতো খোঁজা। proper cope with - পেরে ওঠা: not পচন ধরা, পচা, পচে যাওয়া, hamper, ব্যাহত করা, বাধা দেওয়া, fall victims-শিকার হওয়া productivity-উৎপাদন electricity-বিদ্যুৎ get rotten-পাচ wot get spoiled-নষ্ট হয়ে যাওয়া darkness-wwon sit idiy-অলসভাবে বসে থাকা। go off-বলে যাওয়া candle-, get rid of-মুক্তি পাওয়া necessary steps-প্রয়োজনীয় পদক্ষেপ, ensure-নিশ্চিত করা।",

The ratio of the length and the id the width of the flag is 106. Red and green colours are used in it. The red colour symbolizes the blood of the martyrs and the greet symbolizes that the martyrs who laid down their lives for the freedom of our country are evergreen. Late artit Quamrul Hassan designed it. It is hoisted atop public and private buildings on different national occasions. The national flag is kept half mast on the Martyrs' Day on 21 February.         "question": "Answer the following questions to write a paragraph on \"Traffic Jam\".\n\n(3) What is traffic jam?\n\n(b) What are the causes of traffic jam?(c) What is the effect of traffic jam?\n\n(d) When does generally a traffic jam occur?\n\n(e) How can traffic jam be removed?",
        "solution": "Traffic jam is a crowded mass of vehicles on roads that makes movement difficult or impossible. It is a great nuisance for the modern society. It causes unspeakable sufferings for city or town dwellers. Many vehicles moving on the same road at the same time cause traffic jam. Besides, many of the traffic police are not sincere. They are not inclined to do their duties honestly. Drivers are indifferent to traffic rules. They want to get more and more passengers stopping buses here and there. All these things together cause traffic jam. Moreover, the unlimited number of rickshaws plying on streets is another cause of traffic jam. Generally traffic jam occurs in the morning when students and workers go to their respective destinations and in the afternoon and evening when they retum home. It kills our valuable time. Students often fail to attend classes in time, workers get late at their workplaces and patients have to suffer indescribable sufferings due to traffic jam.         "solution": "All our surroundings including air, water, soil, trees and animals make up our environment. When the normal relations among these elements of nature are disturbed, the ecological balance is hampered and it is called environment pollution. The smoke from factories and motor vehicles contains harmful substances like carbon monoxide oxide and sulfur-di-oxide. These liamper the cleanliness of the air. Mills and factories set up by river banks let out chemical wastes in the river water. These poisonous substances are destroying the plants and creatures of the water bodies. Pesticides and chemical fertilizers used in agriculture are also polluting water. When people drink this water or take a bath in the polluted water, they are attacked with stomach diseases. Environmental pollution may be controlled by taking different measures. We may increase afforestation. If trees are planted in large numbers, we can be benefited in different ways. Trees also increase rainfall and prevent air pollution. Laws should be enacted and implemented to prevent factories from dumping wastes. এইসব একসাথে পরিবেশ গঠন করে। এসব উপাদান মিলেই জীবন চালুর জন্য প্রয়োজনীয় শর্ত বজায় রাখে, তাই এগুলোকে আলাদা ভাবে চিহ্নিত করা হয়। \n\n\u003Cspan class=\"cq-explanation-label\"\u003Eগ\u003C/span\u003E উপাদানগুলো কিভাবে দূষিত হচ্ছে — শিল্পকারখানা ও যানবাহনের ধোঁয়া বায়ুকে দূষিত করে, কলকারখানা ও অপরিষ্কার নিকাশির পানি নদী-সমুদ্র দূষণ করে, পলিথিন ও পচনশীল বর্জ্য মাটি দূষিত করে, আর কীটনাশক ও ভারী ধাতু জীবজগতের মধ্যে জমে ক্ষতি করে। এই উৎসগুলোতে মানুষের কার্যক্রম প্রধান ভূমিকা রাখে, তাই প্রতিটি উপাদান ভিন্ন পথে ক্ষতিগ্রস্ত হয়। \n\n\u003Cspan class=\"cq-explanation-label\"\u003Eঘ\u003C/span\u003E দূষণের প্রভাব — দূষণ স্বাস্থ্যের খারাপ (শ্বাসকষ্ট, জলজ রোগ), খাদ্য ও জলের সংকট, জীববৈচিত্র্যের হ্রাস ও জলবায়ু পরিবর্তন সৃষ্টি করে;         "question": "Write a paragraph on 'The Life of a Farmer' by answering the following questions.\n\na) Who is a farmer? b) When does he start his daily work? c) How does he lead his life? d) What is his contribution to the nation? e) How can we improve his condition?",
        "solution": "[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] Our School MagazineAny person who is involved in the cultivation of crops, or livestock is called a farmer. He gets up early in the morning and starts his daily works. Generally, a farmer is a poor man. Most of the farmers have no land of their own. So, he cultivates the land of others. He lives from hand to mouth. He works very hard to prepare the land for planting or sowing crops. From the farmers' growing and reaping the harvest, we can have our food. By working hard in the field, he grows a bumper crop which helps to develop our national economy. We know that our country is an agricultural country. More than 80 percent people are directly or indirectly engaged in agriculture. Our economy is also mostly dependent on it. So, to promote the development of the national economy, the farmers should be helped with agricultural subsidies by the government. How do the animals and birds pass this day? (d) What do the children do on this day? (e) How do you pass the day?",
        "solution": "[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] A Rainy DayA rainy day is dull and gloomy. Sometimes, it drizzles and sometimes, it rains heavily all day long. The sky remains overcast with black clouds. The sun is hardly visible. Gusty wind blows from all sides. Birds keep standing on branches of trees or keep quiet in their nests. Cattle remain in their sheds and bellow for the fodder. Water stands here and there. Unpitched roads become muddy and slippery. Passers-by have to walk with umbrella over their head, shoes in hand and pants folded up to the knee. Sometimes people slip and fall on the muddy road. In cities, a rainy day is now a horror. The roads and streets in some towns and cities get flooded. Vehicles are seen stranding in knee-deep water in some areas due to water clogging. It causes gridlock across the city. It is a day of trouble and annoyance to the office-going people. They have to suffer from various inconveniences. But for the school going children, it is a delight to have a rainy day. If it rains heavily before their school time, they get a holiday. Sometimes, children, especially the boys play football in the rainwater in the nearby fields. A rainy day is a curse for the poor. The day labourers cannot go out for work and hence, they have to suffer a lot. However, I pass the day by listening to music, watching TV or reading journals. In short, a rainy day is a a day of both pleasure and pain.Word Meaning: dull and gloomy (phr) – নিষ্প্রভ এবং বিষণ্ণ; drizzle (v) গুঁড়ি গুঁড়ি বৃষ্টি হওয়া; overcast (adj) – মেঘাচ্ছন্ন; visible (adj) - দৃশ্যমান; gusty (adj) ঝড়ো; fodder (n) গবাদি পশুর শুকনা খাদ্য; water clogging (phr) – জলাবদ্ধতা; annoyance (n) - বিরক্তি; inconvenience (n) - অসুবিধা; journal (n) সংবাদপত্র/সাময়িক পত্র; In short (phr) - এক কথায়/সংক্ষেপে।",

Sometimes, he sells various items like toys, clothes, fruits, vegetables, and so on. He shouts the names of the items he sells. Children are fond of him because sometimes he wears a strange dress, sings songs or plays on a flute. He walks along the roads and streets from dawn to dusk. He is a man of dignity because he earns his bread through his honest toil. The service that a street hawker does to our society is simply great. He presents the goods that we need daily before our house. He sells his goods at cheaper rates. But sometimes he cheats on simple customers. So we should be careful of the street hawkers who are cheaters. He lives from hand to mouth and leads a simple life. Mostly he lives in a slum.         "question": "Answer the following questions to write a paragraph on \"Tree plantation\":\n\n(a) What does a tree do for us?\n\n(b) What happens if there were no trees?\n\n(c) What is the effect of the loss of trees?\n\n(d) What should be done to save mankind?\n\n(e) How can be made the earth greener, cleaner and safer?\n\n(f) What part do people play in protecting trees and increasing forests?",
        "solution": "[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] Tree Plantation (বৃক্ষরোপণ)Nowadays \"tree plantation' has become a much ventilated issue. \"Tree plantation' means planting trees in a large number to prevent deforestation. The importance of tree plantation beggars description. Firstly, trees provide us with various fruits, honey, fodder for animals, and medicine. Secondly, they supply timber which is used in housing, in making furniture, toys and vehicles, and in manufacturing paper and pencils. Thirdly. almost all the birds and many animals depend on trees for their habitat. Fourthly, trees play the key-role in protecting our environment and maintaining ecological balance. They prevent erosion of soil and protect houses from flood and storm. They absorb carbon-di-oxide, a major culprit for green-house effect. They help rain to occur. Random felling of trees may cause rapid desertification. In recent times, the importance of tree plantation is being desperately felt because our environment is facing increasing threats day by day. Temperature is ever on the rise; polar ice is melting and sea-level is rising; yield of crops are collapsing and so on. July and August are the best time for tree plantation. To motivate people for tree plantation, mass-awareness should be raised. Fallow or unused land available anywhere namely roadsides, sea-beaches. riversides, different institutions etc. can be brought under tree plantation. To conclude, every possible step should be taken for tree plantation until it is too late.Selected Vocabulary (নির্বাচিত শব্দার্থ): Ventilated-আলোচিত; beggar description- বর্ণনাতীত হওয়া; fodder- গবাদি পশুর শুকনা খাদ্য, বিচালি: timber- কাঠ: habitat- আবাস/বাসস্থান; ecological- বাস্তুতান্ত্রিক, পরিবেশগত: culprit- দায়ী, দোষী, random- নির্বিচার, এলোপাতাড়ি, বেপরোয়া, desertification- মরুকরণ; desperately- মরিয়াভাবে, বেপরোয়াভাবে, ব্যাপকভাবে, নিদারুণভাবে: polar-মেরুসম্বন্ধীয়; yield- প্রাকৃতিক রীতিতে উৎপাদন করা বা হওয়া: collapse- ধ্বসে পড়া, ভেঙে পড়া; mass-awareness-জনসচেতনতা; fell-কাটা, (গাছ) কেটে ফেলা; erosion-ক্ষয়; green house-effect- গ্রীন হাউস প্রতিক্রিয়া; motivate- উদ্বুদ্ধ করা; too late- বেশি দেরি; fallow-পতিত (জমি)।",

        "explanation": "Deforestation is the large-scale clearing of forests for other land uses. Its main causes are agricultural expansion (both subsistence and commercial), logging for timber and fuel, urbanization, infrastructure and mining. Cutting trees removes vegetation that holds soil and water, so it increases erosion, reduces soil fertility, disrupts local water cycles and destroys habitats, causing biodiversity loss and forcing animals and people to migrate. Trees store carbon; when they are felled or burned, that carbon is released as greenhouse gases, which alters climate—this link makes deforestation a global problem because local forest loss contributes to global warming and affects weather patterns worldwide. Preventing deforestation requires legal protection of forests, sustainable forest management, reforestation and agroforestry, economic incentives for conservation, and consumer choices that avoid products linked to forest clearing; combining policy, community action and market measures balances development with forest conservation.",

        "question": "Answering the following questions to write a paragraph on 'Water Pollution' :\n\n(a) What is water pollution?\n\n(b) Why is water called life?\n\n(c) How is water polluted?\n\n(d) What are the effects of water pollution?\n\n(e) What measures should we take to prevent water pollution?",
        "solution": "Water is an essential element of environment. No one can live without water. This is why water is called life. But nowadays it is being polluted in many ways. This pollution of water through various ways is called water pollution. Different kinds of human waste fall into water through unplanned drainage system. Chemicals and fertilizers used by farmers and industrial waste pollute water. Engine vehicles using fossil fuels ply the rivers and seas, and leave oil and waste materials into water. As a result, water is polluted. Thermal pollution and radio-active wastage are also responsible. The effects of water pollution are numerous because it triggers imbalance in the entire environment and becomes the cause of many diseases. Every year diarrhoea, cholera, typhoid and such other diseases breaking out as a result of water pollution cause millions of deaths in the world. To prevent water pollution, we should leave no stone unturned and have to check all the culprits responsible for it. Proper dumping of all sorts of waste is the most effective step here. Sanitary latrines should be introduced widely in the river-side areas. Passing as well as enforcing a law against dumping of waste into water is sure to be fruitful. In fact, preventing water pollution is a crying need for us, because it harms the acquatic life and, after all, the entire environment.\n\nSelected vocabulary (নির্বাচিত পদার্থ) Leave no stone unturned চৌটার কোনো ত্রুটি না করা: as a result ফলে, ফলতিতে।introduce- পরিচয় করিয়ে দেওয়া। prevent- রোর করা, প্রতিরোধ করা; crying need- অতীব প্রয়োজন, unplanned- অপরিকল্পিত। drainage systeen- বষয়শন প্রক্রিয়া। fossil- জীবাশ্ম। ply- চলাচল করা thermal- বাণী: radio-active coafse, dump -বোঝা নামানো: আবর্জনার সুখ acquatic source- environment-পরিবেশঃ pollute-দৃষিresponsible-থায়ী; clement-উপাদান। check-প্রতিহত করা, দমন করা: effective-কার্যকর, proper-উপযুক্ত, widely-ব্যাপকভাবে enfoনয়ে-প্রয়োগ করা, কার্যকরী fruitful-ফলদায়ক, harm-স্বতি করা।",

But usually in a tea stall some more light items like biscuits, bananas, breads and cigarettes are also sold. So, a tea stall is also a stall of light food. A tea stall is found at a market place, a square, a bus stand, a railway station and near schools and colleges. Though some stalls are well fumished, most of the tea stalls are poorly furnished with furniture. People go to a tea stall to take a cup of tea in order to remove tiredness. They go there almost all day long. To serve them, a tea stall is kept open from early morning till late night. In a tea stall there are usually two people to manage and run it. One is a grown up man who prepares tea and takes bill from the customers, and another is a young boy who serves tea, biscuits etc. to the clients. Sometimes, people come to a tea stall in a group and raise a storm over the cup. They discuss harvest, market prices of daily necessaries and politics. A tea stall becomes more vibrant during elections.         "question": "Answer the following questions to write a paragraph on \"Environment Pollution\" .\n\n(a)What is Environment pollution?\n\n(b) What are the elements of the \"Environment'?\n\n(c) How are the elements of Environment being polluted?\n\n(d) What is the effect of pollution?\n\n(e) How are people responsible for environment pollution?\n\n(1) What should we do to stop environment pollution?",
        "solution": "All our surroundings including air, water, soil, trees and animals make up our environment. When the normal relations among these elements of nature are disturbed, the ecological balance is hampered and it is called environment pollution. The smoke from factories and motor vehicles contains harmful substances like carbon monoxide oxide and sulfur-di-oxide. These liamper the cleanliness of the air. Mills and factories set up by river banks let out chemical wastes in the river water. These poisonous substances are destroying the plants and creatures of the water bodies. Pesticides and chemical fertilizers used in agriculture are also polluting water. When people drink this water or take a bath in the polluted water, they are attacked with stomach diseases. Environmental pollution may be controlled by taking different measures. We may increase afforestation. If trees are planted in large numbers, we can be benefited in different ways.         "question": "Answer the following questions to write a paragraph on \"Traffic Jam\".\n\n(3) What is traffic jam?\n\n(b) What are the causes of traffic jam?(c) What is the effect of traffic jam?\n\n(d) When does generally a traffic jam occur?\n\n(e) How can traffic jam be removed?",
        "solution": "Traffic jam is a crowded mass of vehicles on roads that makes movement difficult or impossible. It is a great nuisance for the modern society. It causes unspeakable sufferings for city or town dwellers. Many vehicles moving on the same road at the same time cause traffic jam. Besides, many of the traffic police are not sincere. They are not inclined to do their duties honestly. Drivers are indifferent to traffic rules. They want to get more and more passengers stopping buses here and there. All these things together cause traffic jam. Moreover, the unlimited number of rickshaws plying on streets is another cause of traffic jam. Generally traffic jam occurs in the morning when students and workers go to their respective destinations and in the afternoon and evening when they retum home. It kills our valuable time. Students often fail to attend classes in time, workers get late at their workplaces and patients have to suffer indescribable sufferings due to traffic jam. This nuisance should not be allowed to continue. Strict law should be imposed to control traffic jam. Exemplary punishment should be given to the drivers who do not obey the traffic rules. It causes unspeakable sufferings for city or town dwellers. Many vehicles moving on the same road at the same time cause traffic jam. Besides, many of the traffic police are not sincere. They are not inclined to do their duties honestly. Drivers are indifferent to traffic rules. They want to get more and more passengers stopping buses here and there. All these things together cause traffic jam. Moreover, the unlimited number of rickshaws plying on streets is another cause of traffic jam. Generally traffic jam occurs in the morning when students and workers go to their respective destinations and in the afternoon and evening when they retum home. It kills our valuable time. Sometimes, he sells various items like toys, clothes, fruits, vegetables, and so on. He shouts the names of the items he sells. Children are fond of him because sometimes he wears a strange dress, sings songs or plays on a flute. He walks along the roads and streets from dawn to dusk. He is a man of dignity because he earns his bread through his honest toil. The service that a street hawker does to our society is simply great. He presents the goods that we need daily before our house. He sells his goods at cheaper rates. But sometimes he cheats on simple customers. So we should be careful of the street hawkers who are cheaters. He lives from hand to mouth and leads a simple life. Mostly he lives in a slum. They attract customers by calling out, displaying items on portable carts or trays, offering samples and low prices — these methods work because hawkers have little capital and rely on quick, visible sales to earn money.         "solution": "Traffic jam is a situation in which a long line of vehicles on a road stop moving or move very slowly. Nowadays, traffic jam is a common problem in our towns and cities. It causes great sufferings to the passengers and the passers-by. The increasing number of vehicles mostly causes traffic jam. Day by day, the number of vehicles is increasing to meet the needs of the increased population. But the roads are not increasing in that proportion. Many vehicles moving on the same road at a time cause traffic jam. Many drivers do not abide by traffic rules. Besides, the traffic police are not sincere. The tendency of the bus drivers and conductors to get more passengers also causes traffic jam. Sonie drivers stop buses here and there and board and unboard passengers. This hampers the movement of other vehicles and causes traffic jam. The unlimited number of rickshaws plying on the streets is another cause of traffic jam. The general people have to face untold sufferings. They reach late at their working places. Students, employees, businessmen, workers all suffer tremendously for this. It occurs mostly during office and school or college time. During traffic jam, we feel extremely bored as it kills our valuable time. To relieve the passengers of the sufferings of traffic jam, some steps should be taken by the government. The drivers who do not abide by traffic rules should be punished.         "solution": "[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] Our School MagazineA school magazine is a periodical publication that contains the literary works and other information of a school. It is published once a year. We have a school magazine in our school. To publish it smoothly, a magazine committee of usually nine members is formed in a general meeting. The members of the committee are chief patron, adviser, editor, assistant editors, business editors, proofreaders, assistant proofreaders, etc. The Headteacher holds the post of chief patron and a senior teacher becomes the adviser. The editor, business editors and the assistant proofreaders are selected from the students. A magazine fund is also made up from the school 'Magazine Fee'. The editor invites writings both in Bangla and English. Then, after proper scrutiny, the best ones are selected for publishing. The business editors collect some money by selling spaces in the magazine for advertisements. Generally, the magazine has two sections- Bangla and English. There are messages from the Headteacher and the Secretary of the school. There are also annual reports, essays, short stories, short plays, etc. in it. It also contains jokes, quizes and puzzles. Most of the articles are written by the students. A few articles are written by the teachers. A school magazine promoting team-spirit inspires to express the dormant power of thinking as well as writing of the young learners. It helps flourish themselves as future writers and poets.Word Meaning: contain (v) - ধারণ করা/থাকা; literary (adj) সাহিত্য বিষয়ক; information (n) – তথ্য; smoothly (adv) - মসৃণভাবে; form (v) - গঠন করা; patron (n) পৃষ্ঠপোষক; adviser (n) - উপদেষ্টা; editor (n) সম্পাদক; invite (v) - আহ্বান করা; proper (adj) - যথাযথ; scrutiny (n) বিচার বিশ্লেষণ; select (v) নির্বাচন করা; collect (v) সংগ্রহ করা; promote (v) - উন্নীত করা/প্রচার করা; inspire (v) অনুপ্রাণিত করা; express (v) প্রকাশ করা; flourish (v) - বিকশিত করা।",

        "solution": "Early rising is a positive habit. It means that we should get up from bed early in the morning to enable ourselves to be ready for a new day. This fact, when made into a regular habit, will surely lead us to a world of bliss and prosperity. A proverb says, \"Early to bed and early to rise makes a man healthy, wealthy and wise.\" Early rising has many benefits. The man who rises early in the morning can take some exercises or a walk in the fresh air by the riverside or in the open field. It makes our minds fresh and lively. Early in the morning, nature seems quiet and calm. No hue and cry are heard then. Nature smiles in the morning with colourful flowers and green leaves. Birds begin to chirp. These beautiful gifts and colourful nature in the morning remind everybody of the Creator. One feels like praying to the Almighty. But it is not easy to attain this quality. Sleeping late at night does not help in early rising. So, to rise early from bed, we have to go to bed early. An early riser enjoys the surroundings very much and gets enough time to do his work either in study or in other work, which will bring him success. On the contrary, if one gets up late, the schedule of his work becomes interrupted. Above all, early rising keeps us healthy and cheerful. For all these reasons, we all should cultivate the habit of early rising.",

This is correct because it emphasizes shifting wake time earlier to gain morning hours.\n\n(b) It benefits health by aligning sleep with natural circadian rhythms, providing more exposure to morning light, improving digestion and metabolism, and allowing time for exercise and calm start—actions that collectively boost physical and mental well‑being. These points explain why early rising has measurable health effects.\n\n(c) For students it is important because early mornings offer quiet, uninterrupted time for study, better concentration, regular routines, and sufficient sleep when bedtime is kept consistent—factors that improve learning and academic performance. This shows how timing and routine aid study habits.\n\n(d) Early rising also increases productivity and time management, reduces rush and stress, creates space for exercise or planning, and fosters punctuality and self‑discipline. These practical benefits explain its broader positive impact on daily life.\n\n(e) To form the habit, keep a consistent bedtime, shift wake time gradually (for example 15 minutes earlier every few days), avoid screens before bed, use a fixed morning routine, and be persistent. People cut down trees and use them as fuel in houses and industries. To meet the extra need of the extra population, forests are cut down and used for agriculture and habitat. It is a great threat to human existence on earth. It threatens wildlife and even the very existence of the planet. Removal of trees compel binds and animals living on them to change their habitat and it hampers their normal life and breeding. Deforestation is a menacing threat to ecological balance. Due to deforestation, greenhouse effect is worsening day by day. The world temperature is increasing, sea-level is rising, yield of crop is decreasing and rapid, desertification is occurring in many places. Deforestation causes great damage to the soil. Finally the soil gets sedimented in the riverbed and causes flood. Deforestation also causes drought and harms agriculture. It is so great a threat that it should not be allowed to go on any further, Mass-awareness about the issue should be raised. More and more trees should be planted.         "solution": "[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] Tree Plantation (বৃক্ষরোপণ)Nowadays \"tree plantation' has become a much ventilated issue. \"Tree plantation' means planting trees in a large number to prevent deforestation. The importance of tree plantation beggars description. Firstly, trees provide us with various fruits, honey, fodder for animals, and medicine. Secondly, they supply timber which is used in housing, in making furniture, toys and vehicles, and in manufacturing paper and pencils. Thirdly. almost all the birds and many animals depend on trees for their habitat. Fourthly, trees play the key-role in protecting our environment and maintaining ecological balance. They prevent erosion of soil and protect houses from flood and storm. They absorb carbon-di-oxide, a major culprit for green-house effect. They help rain to occur. Random felling of trees may cause rapid desertification. In recent times, the importance of tree plantation is being desperately felt because our environment is facing increasing threats day by day. Temperature is ever on the rise; polar ice is melting and sea-level is rising; yield of crops are collapsing and so on. July and August are the best time for tree plantation. To motivate people for tree plantation, mass-awareness should be raised. Fallow or unused land available anywhere namely roadsides, sea-beaches. riversides, different institutions etc. can be brought under tree plantation. To conclude, every possible step should be taken for tree plantation until it is too late.Selected Vocabulary (নির্বাচিত শব্দার্থ): Ventilated-আলোচিত; beggar description- বর্ণনাতীত হওয়া; fodder- গবাদি পশুর শুকনা খাদ্য, বিচালি: timber- কাঠ: habitat- আবাস/বাসস্থান; ecological- বাস্তুতান্ত্রিক, পরিবেশগত: culprit- দায়ী, দোষী, random- নির্বিচার, এলোপাতাড়ি, বেপরোয়া, desertification- মরুকরণ; desperately- মরিয়াভাবে, বেপরোয়াভাবে, ব্যাপকভাবে, নিদারুণভাবে: polar-মেরুসম্বন্ধীয়; yield- প্রাকৃতিক রীতিতে উৎপাদন করা বা হওয়া: collapse- ধ্বসে পড়া, ভেঙে পড়া; mass-awareness-জনসচেতনতা; fell-কাটা, (গাছ) কেটে ফেলা; erosion-ক্ষয়; green house-effect- গ্রীন হাউস প্রতিক্রিয়া; motivate- উদ্বুদ্ধ করা; too late- বেশি দেরি; fallow-পতিত (জমি)।",

It is found in a marketplace, a square, a bus stand, a railway station and near schools and colleges. In a tea stall, usually, tea is served to the customers in exchange for money. But biscuits, bananas, cigarettes, betel leaves, etc. are also sold there. Though some tea stalls are well-furnished, most of them are poorly furnished. It is usually decorated with chairs, tables and benches. People go to a tea stall to take a cup of tea to remove their tiredness. A tea stall is kept open from early morning till late night. In a tea stall, there are generally two people to manage and run it. One is a grown-up man who prepares tea and takes the bill from the customers, and the other is a young boy who serves tea, biscuits, etc. to the customers.         "question": "Answer the following questions to write a paragraph on 'Your School Magazine'.\n\na) What is a school magazine? b) What is the name of your school magazine? c) How is the magazine committee formed? d) What does it contain? e) What is the importance of a school magazine?",
        "solution": "[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] Our School MagazineA school magazine is a periodical publication that contains the literary works and other information of a school. It is published once a year. We have a school magazine in our school. To publish it smoothly, a magazine committee of usually nine members is formed in a general meeting. The members of the committee are chief patron, adviser, editor, assistant editors, business editors, proofreaders, assistant proofreaders, etc. The Headteacher holds the post of chief patron and a senior teacher becomes the adviser. The editor, business editors and the assistant proofreaders are selected from the students. A magazine fund is also made up from the school 'Magazine Fee'. The editor invites writings both in Bangla and English. Then, after proper scrutiny, the best ones are selected for publishing. The business editors collect some money by selling spaces in the magazine for advertisements. Generally, the magazine has two sections- Bangla and English. There are messages from the Headteacher and the Secretary of the school. There are also annual reports, essays, short stories, short plays, etc. in it. It also contains jokes, quizes and puzzles. Most of the articles are written by the students. A few articles are written by the teachers. He gets up early in the morning and starts his daily works. Generally, a farmer is a poor man. Most of the farmers have no land of their own. So, he cultivates the land of others. He lives from hand to mouth. He works very hard to prepare the land for planting or sowing crops. From the farmers' growing and reaping the harvest, we can have our food. By working hard in the field, he grows a bumper crop which helps to develop our national economy. We know that our country is an agricultural country. More than 80 percent people are directly or indirectly engaged in agriculture. Our economy is also mostly dependent on it. So, to promote the development of the national economy, the farmers should be helped with agricultural subsidies by the government. They should be encouraged to use tractors instead of the age-old ploughs. They should also be taught to use modern cultivation methods. This is how the farmers can be developed.Word Meaning: land জমি; prepare প্রস্তুত করা; crops ফসল; bumper ব্যাপক; economy অর্থনীতি; agricultural কৃষিপ্রধান; directly প্রত্যক্ষভাবে; dependent নির্ভরশীল; subsidies ভর্তুকি; instead পরিবর্তে; modern আধুনিক; cultivation - চাষাবাদ; methods - পদ্ধতি।",

        "question": "Write a paragraph on 'A Rainy Day' answering the following questions: (a) Hów is a rainy day? (b) What happens in the rainy season? (c) What do people do on this day? How do the animals and birds pass this day? (d) What do the children do on this day? (e) How do you pass the day?",
        "solution": "[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] A Rainy DayA rainy day is dull and gloomy. Sometimes, it drizzles and sometimes, it rains heavily all day long. The sky remains overcast with black clouds. The sun is hardly visible. Gusty wind blows from all sides. Birds keep standing on branches of trees or keep quiet in their nests. Cattle remain in their sheds and bellow for the fodder. Water stands here and there. Unpitched roads become muddy and slippery. Passers-by have to walk with umbrella over their head, shoes in hand and pants folded up to the knee. Sometimes people slip and fall on the muddy road. In cities, a rainy day is now a horror. The roads and streets in some towns and cities get flooded. Vehicles are seen stranding in knee-deep water in some areas due to water clogging. It causes gridlock across the city. It is a day of trouble and annoyance to the office-going people. They have to suffer from various inconveniences. But for the school going children, it is a delight to have a rainy day. If it rains heavily before their school time, they get a holiday. Sometimes, children, especially the boys play football in the rainwater in the nearby fields. A rainy day is a curse for the poor. The day labourers cannot go out for work and hence, they have to suffer a lot. However, I pass the day by listening to music, watching TV or reading journals. In short, a rainy day is a a day of both pleasure and pain.Word Meaning: dull and gloomy (phr) – নিষ্প্রভ এবং বিষণ্ণ; drizzle (v) গুঁড়ি গুঁড়ি বৃষ্টি হওয়া; overcast (adj) – মেঘাচ্ছন্ন; visible (adj) - দৃশ্যমান; gusty (adj) ঝড়ো; fodder (n) গবাদি পশুর শুকনা খাদ্য; water clogging (phr) – জলাবদ্ধতা; annoyance (n) - বিরক্তি; inconvenience (n) - অসুবিধা; journal (n) সংবাদপত্র/সাময়িক পত্র; In short (phr) - এক কথায়/সংক্ষেপে।",

Other uses of smartphone are making phone call, listening to music, using social media apps, capturing and sharing photos and videos, etc. The effects of Smart phone on human life is huge. At present, there is hardly any person who doesn't have a smartphone. Smart phone has enabled us to communicate with the people of the whole world in an instant. It has facilitated our life to a great extent. But alongside the huge number of benefits that we get from smart phone, it also brings about some troubles in our life.         "solution": "[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] A Street AccidentThe accident that occurs on the streets due to face to face collision, break-failure or strong dash back of buses, trucks or any two other vehicles is called street accident. Last Sunday, I witnessed a tragic street accident. It took place near our school. There is a turning there. It is an interchange of five roads. Now and then, there occurs a traffic jam. On that day, while I was going to school, I saw a car coming from the western direction. A rickshaw, with a school boy and his mother, was coming from the opposite direction at about 8:30 a.m. While crossing the point, the car hit the rickshaw. The rickshawpuller was able to jump from his seat but the boy and his mother fell on the street. The boy and his mother were seriously wounded. I rushed to them. Some other passers-by also came forward to help them. We led them to a nearby doctor's chamber. I felt pity for the school boy, he was of my age. In fact, for having no traffic police at that place, such accidents frequently occur.         "question": "Answer the following questions to write a paragraph on \"Load Shedding\".\n\na) What does the term 'load shedding' mean?\n\nb) What are the causes of load shedding?\n\nc) How does it hamper us?\n\nd) How can this problem be solved?",
        "solution": "Load shedding means the disruption of power supply due to extra load. In other words, load shedding is to stop the supply of electricity when the demand is more than the supply. Sometimes the necessity of electricity surpasses the amount of its supply. At that time, the production is less than the actual demand. It becomes impossible to supply electricity to all areas due to the shortage. So, the electricity supply authority stops supplying electricity for a short period to some areas by turns in order to ensure balarice between the supply and demand. As a result, load shedding occurs to some areas. Load shedding causes a lot of problems. It occurs without any notice. So, it disrupts running mills and factories. For that, the production is hampered. It causes harm to machineries. Emergency medical treatment in hospitals is badly affected. Computer users lose unsaved data. Study of students is greatly hampered, and they suffer a lot. In a word, all the activities related to electricity are hindered due to load shedding.         "question": "(a) What is deforestation? (b) What are the causes of deforestation? (c) What are the impacts of deforestation on human being, fauna, nature and climate? (d) How will the low-lying countries be affected? (e) How can deforestation be prevented?",
        "solution": "[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math]Deforestation (নির্বনায়ন)Deforestation means the act of cutting down or burning the trees indiscriminately in an area. Nowadays it has become a global problem. There are many causes of deforestation. Among them, population explosion is the main cause of deforestation. People use wood for different purpose. They need shelter, agricultural land, fuel, furniture, etc. For all these reasons people cut trees. There are many impacts of deforestation on human being, fauna, nature and climate. If people cut down trees at random, one day a number of regions will turn into deserts. There will be no rain and as a result, agriculture will face a great crisis. The global temperature will rise and it will cause Greenhouse Effect. The sea level will rise and the low-lying countries of the world will go under water. Moreover, deforestation leads to many ecologically damaging outcomes affecting the flora and fauna of the area, and disturbing the food chain and the hydrological cycle. So, we should prevent deforestation. To get rid of this problem, social awareness can be raised regarding bad effects of deforestation. For this. purpose, tree plantation programme can be raised through print and electronic media. Besides, strict laws should be made and implemented to reduce deforestation. After all, if we want to save our planet, we must protect our forests.Word Meaning (শব্দার্থ): indiscriminately-নির্বিচারে। global problem-বৈশ্বিক সমস্যা। population explosion-জনবিস্ফোরণ। shelter- আশ্রয়। impact-প্রভাব। climate-জলবায়ু। crisis-সংকট। greenhouse effect-গ্রীনহাউজ প্রভাব। ecologyically-পরিবেশগতভাবে। damaging-ক্ষতিকর। hydrological cyycle-জলবিজ্ঞানসংক্রান্ত চক্র। prevent-প্রতিরোধ করা। get rid of-মুক্তি পাওয়া। social awareness -সামাজিক সচেতনতা। raise-বাড়ানো। implement-প্রয়োগ করা। protect-রক্ষা করা।",
